Identifying those records which has Null values in the both columns Reaction Type & User ID. We will remove such records from this dataset, and keeping records which has only UserID missing or no missing values in other columns.¶
In [35]:
col_list=['Score']
In [36]:
def treat_missing_values_num(col_list, data):
    
    for i in col_list:
        col_name = i
        print('Independent Variable: ',col_name)
        print('Check if there are any missing value in variable',col_name,': ')
        if (data[col_name].isnull().any().any() == True):
            print('No. of Observations with missing value: ', data[col_name].isnull().sum(axis=0))
            # Replacing missing values with Median
            data[col_name].fillna(data[col_name].median(), inplace=True)
            print('After treating the missing values')
            print(data[col_name].isnull().sum(axis=0))
            print('')
        else:
            print('No missing values found in ',col_name)
            print('')

for idx in user_data.index:
    device = user_data['Device'][idx]
    age = user_data['Age'][idx]
    user_id = user_data['User ID'][idx]
    print(idx)
    print(device)
    print(age)
    print(user_id)
    for i in content_data.index:
        if (content_data['User ID'][i] == user_id):
            content_data['Device'][i] = device
            content_data['User Age'][i] = age
